### [88] [The Perplexity Trap: When Patent Law Makes Human Writing Look Like AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13044)
*Anubhab Banerjee*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文分析了在资源受限（消费级GPU）环境下，欧专局最新政策推动下，现有主流AI文本检测器在专利文本场景中的表现，并提出了一种基于语言复杂度特征的方法提升检测准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 2026年EPO新指南要求申请人对AI辅助生成内容负责，催生对可疑AI生成专利文本的筛查需求。然而，专利申请审查往往资源有限，大部分只能使用8GB VRAM的消费级GPU。此外，专利权利要求书本身需保持低困惑度和低突发性，与LLMs生成文本特征高度重合，导致现有检测方法容易误判。

Method: 作者对比了三种开源零样本（zero-shot）AI生成文本检测器，在500份真实EPO H04专利和500份LLM生成的专利文本（含5种不同prompt策略）上评测，在消费级硬件上实现。额外还在其他专利分类、模型（如Qwen2.5-3B、Pythia-2.8B等）上做了广泛测试。同时提出并测试了一种基于七项语言复杂度特征的逻辑回归方法，无需推理阶段likelihood计算。

Result: 现有主流检测器如Binoculars、Fast-DetectGPT、DetectGPT在claim级别的误报率高达61.3-80.5%。几乎所有横向扩展测试（模型/领域/硬件）都显示高误报是结构性问题。提出的七特征语言复杂度线性模型准确率提升至74.0%，FPR降至28.1%，比仅用困惑度特征提升约13个百分点，且计算资源需求不变。

Conclusion: 针对EPO专利写作场景，现有AI生成文本检测器普遍失效，主要受专利文本固有特性影响。基于语言复杂度的轻量级机器学习方法能显著减少误报，更适用实践部署，但检测问题本身在结构上仍具挑战性。

Abstract: The European Patent Office (EPO) reported record filings in 2025, and the 2026 EPO Guidelines hold applicants strictly responsible for LLM-assisted content under Article 83 and Rule 42, creating pressure to triage suspected AI-generated patent text. Two constraints make this hard. First, realistic prosecution settings often have only consumer GPUs with about 8 GB VRAM, not datacenter-class scoring stacks. Second, Article 84 of the European Patent Convention requires claims to be clear and concise, pushing human drafting onto the same low-perplexity, low-burstiness manifold that LLMs occupy. We benchmark three open-source zero-shot detectors on 500 granted EPO H04 telecom patents versus 500 LLM-generated counterparts using five prompting strategies, all under the consumer hardware envelope. At claim level, all detectors exceed 60 percent false-positive rate: Binoculars 78.3 percent, Fast-DetectGPT 61.3 percent, DetectGPT 80.5 percent. The failure persists under Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct regeneration, LoRA-adapted Pythia-2.8B scoring heads, cross-IPC replication on A61K, C07D, and F03D (mean FPR 84.6 percent), and H100 re-evaluation with published Falcon-7B and GPT-J-6B heads, arguing the issue is structural rather than substitute-model capacity. A seven-feature linguistic-complexity logistic regression reaches 74.0 percent accuracy at 28.1 percent FPR, a 13 percentage-point gain over a perplexity-only baseline at a comparable operating point, without using likelihood at inference and within the same hardware budget.

### [89] [Do LLMs Need Architectural Changes for Simultaneous Speech Translation? A Prefix-to-Prefix Data Driven Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13158)
*Junkun Chen,Jian Xue,Ming Tang,Abdel Heba,Hoda Gholami,Ruchao Fan,Jinyu Li*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有SimulST方法往往依赖模型架构变更或显式的读取/写入策略来平衡延迟和输出，但这些技术在口语场景下因分段边界模糊而不够稳健。为了解决这一痛点，作者寻求一种更简洁、稳健的数据驱动方法。

Method: 作者提出利用固定长度分块进行累积流式译码，并引入基于回退的已提交前缀与有界等待的Prefix-to-Prefix（P2P）标签进行微调。提出了一种新的CSSEL流式语音编码器LLM，并结合P2P监督，实现CSSEL-P2P系统。

Abstract: Simultaneous speech translation (SimulST) requires incremental translation under strict latency constraints, yet remains challenging for decoder-only LLM systems due to limited context and cross-lingual reordering. Recent approaches often introduce architectural changes or explicit read/write policies to control output timing, which can be brittle in conversational speech where segmentation boundaries are ambiguous. We present a simple data-driven alternative: fixed-length chunks for cumulative streaming decoding with a rewind-based committed prefix, and teacher-labeled prefix-to-prefix (P2P) targets with bounded waiting for fine-tuning, yielding CSSEL-P2P, where CSSEL is our proposed chunked streaming speech encoder LLM. In our in-house conversational speech evaluation, CSSEL-P2P improves streaming quality by +1.54 COMETKiwi over the CSSEL streaming baseline at comparable latency (+0.15s Average Lagging), suggesting effective SimulST without architectural changes via P2P supervision.

### [90] [What Models Express, Suppress, and Resist: Auditing Open-Weight LLMs with Persona Vectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13162)
*Winston Zeng,Ali Emami,Jinho Choi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文系统性地利用“人格向量”探索大语言模型（LLM）在多种行为特质上的表达及可调性，发现模型对部分特质天然表达，对部分可被引导放大，亦存在难以提取的特质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前关于LLM行为的研究多限于少数特质，且难以揭示模型藏匿与抗拒行为的内部机制。因此，作者提出用更系统、更广泛的人格向量方法全面梳理和理解模型行为特质的表达和可调空间。

Method: 作者构建了包含53种行为特质的清单，覆盖四个领域，对两款开源大模型的每项特质打标签（如自然表达、可引导放大、难以提取），并进行行为特质组合及可引导测试。还通过范式转移，将微调后的行为向量用于标准模型以观察提取效果。

Result: 两款模型均以助人、任务导向为默认，对应的自然特质与心理专家判断高度一致。可引导提升的特质集中在模型默认不表现的特质上（如夸张、幻觉、阿谀奉承）。若尝试提取“邪恶”等抗拒特质，仅用向量转移才能恢复此行为，且模型在推理链中仍表现出抗拒。

Conclusion: 人格向量不仅能作为控制工具，更能作为揭示大模型行为结构的重要探针，深刻剖析模型特质分布、抵抗与表达机制。

Abstract: What a language model will and will not do is largely set during post-training, but which behaviors it expresses, hides, or resists is not revealed by prompting alone. Persona vectors, behavioral directions in activation space, can probe this organization, but prior work covers only a handful of traits. We present the first systematic application of persona vectors at this scale, compiling a 53-trait inventory across four behaviorally distinct domains and labeling every trait in two open-weight models as natural (expressed at baseline), steerable latent but amplifiable, or intractable (resistant to standard extraction). Both models default to helpful, task-oriented behavior: all nine agentic traits are natural, and their default clinician behavior matches a board-certified psychologist's independent desirability judgments on 16 of 17 traits. Steering produces its largest gains on traits these defaults exclude: hyperbole, hallucination, and sycophancy. The same asymmetry holds across all 171 generic-trait pairs: two steerable traits can collapse the composition, but pairs involving a default never do. Where standard extraction fails on a trait like "evil," a vector transferred from a fine-tuned variant still recovers it, with the residual refusals appearing inside the model's chain-of-thought. Persona vectors are most informative not as a set of controls but as a probe of behavioral organization.

</details>


### [91] [Text2Sign: A Single-GPU Diffusion Baseline for Text-to-Sign Language Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13164)
*Ruize Xia*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Text2Sign的文本驱动手语视频生成扩散模型，可在单块NVIDIA L4 GPU上实现高效推理。通过3D编码器-解码器和分解时空注意力机制，该模型显著降低了成本并保持动作连贯性。模型虽受限于低分辨率短片段，但在资源受限场景下为相关研究提供了有效基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手语是聋人和听障人群的主要交流方式，然而现有的文本到手语视频生成由于扩散模型昂贵，难以在资源有限条件下推广。因此，开发能够在较低硬件需求下运行，并保持生成视频质量的方法具有重要意义。

Method: 提出了Text2Sign扩散模型，结合冻结的视觉-语言文本编码器、3D编码-解码结构以及分解的时空注意力机制。作者比较了不同主干结构（卷积与Transformer）、文本编码方式与注意力策略。

Result: 最佳模型在How2Sign测试集上短周期验证损失达到0.0648，长周期损失降至0.00999。生成32帧低分辨率手语片段用时12.60秒，较低的推理显存需求（3.12GB）。生成视频在保持一定质量同时，还具备很强的时间一致性，但对文本提示的敏感性较弱。

Conclusion: Text2Sign能在单GPU下生成连贯的低分辨率短手语视频，适合作为研究基线，但当前仅支持短片段、低分辨率场景且缺乏语言学专家评测，离实际生产系统还有差距。代码已开源。

Abstract: Sign language is a primary communication channel for millions of Deaf and hard-of-hearing people, yet text-to-signer video generation remains costly because video diffusion models are expensive to train and evaluate. This paper presents Text2Sign, a text-conditioned diffusion model for short sign-language clips that runs on a single NVIDIA L4 GPU. It combines a frozen vision-language text encoder with a 3D encoder-decoder and factorized spatiotemporal attention to reduce the cost of full-video attention while preserving motion coherence.
  We compare convolution-only and transformer-style backbones, frozen pretrained and task-specific text encoders, and factorized versus full attention. On a signer-disjoint How2Sign split, the best short-run ablation reaches a validation loss of 0.0648, while a longer-run checkpoint reaches 0.00999. On a compact evaluation slice, the latter achieves an SSIM of $0.2403 \pm 0.0238$, a PSNR of $15.11 \pm 0.42$ dB, and temporal consistency of $1.0000 \pm 0.0000$ using 8-step DDIM sampling with a guidance scale of 5.0. It generates a 32-frame, $64 \times 64$ clip in 12.60 seconds, or 2.54 frames per second, with peak inference memory of 3.12 GB.
  A held-out denoising audit shows only weak prompt sensitivity: removing text increases late-timestep loss from 0.9875 to 0.9891, while shuffled prompts perform similarly to correct prompts. Frozen text conditioning therefore improves short-budget validation loss, but prompt-specific separation remains limited. The system is restricted to low-resolution, short clips and lacks expert linguistic evaluation, so it should be viewed as a single-GPU research baseline rather than a complete sign-language production system. Code is available at https://github.com/xiaruize0911/text2sign.

</details>


### [92] [RAGthoven at SemEval-2026 Task 1: A Multi-Stage Pipeline Walks Into a Benchmark and Barely Clears the Bar](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13189)
*Marek Šuppa,Viktória Ondrejová,Lucia Ganajová,Gregor Karetka,Daniel Skala*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: RAGthoven系统用于多语言幽默文本生成任务，通过多阶段大模型流程和检索增强生成，在三种语言上与基线模型表现相当。复杂流程带来的提升因语言而异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多语言幽默文本生成任务尚缺有效系统，尤其是结合幽默理论和新一代大模型。研究希望改进模型的创造性输出，并量化复杂生成流程的价值。

Method: 系统分为四步：规划（Planner）、多样化生成（Writer）、自我反思（Reflector）、判定（Judge），各环节结合幽默理论。最终方案引入笑话语料的检索增强生成（RAG），并测试了两种“agentic”自动流程变体，设置了工具调用约束审核器。

Result: 无论采用哪种自动流程，RAGthoven在测试样本上都未明显优于常规流程。最终，该系统与Gemini 2.5 Flash基线在三种语言表现持平。西班牙语表现最好，英语和中文与基线差距不大但在统计置信区间内。

Conclusion: 高阶多阶段提示策略与代理型流程在有强大语言模型基础时，带来的提升有限且多依赖具体语言，提示进一步复杂化流程的边际收益递减。

Abstract: We present RAGthoven, our system for SemEval-2026 Task 1 (MWAHAHA), Subtask A (multilingual constrained humor generation in English, Spanish, and Chinese). RAGthoven decomposes creative text generation into a multi-stage large language model (LLM) pipeline (Planner, Best-of-N Writer, Reflector for self-critique, LLM-as-a-judge Judge) grounded in computational humor theory (Benign Violation Theory, Script-based Semantic Theory of Humor) and refined across ten experiments.
  In our final configuration, we augment the Planner with retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) from a curated joke corpus, seeding generation with diverse joke mechanisms. We also evaluate two agentic variants -- ReAct-style sequential tool-calling (Exp09) and autonomous multi-branch orchestration (Exp10) -- that expose the same four stages with a deterministic ConstraintAudit checker. Across four frontier models on a held-out 12-instance English sample, neither agentic variant produced outputs we judged superior to the non-agentic pipeline despite substantially higher tool-call budgets.
  RAGthoven shares Rank 1 with the Gemini 2.5 Flash baseline in all three languages, with overlapping organizer-reported confidence intervals. In Spanish, it leads the baseline by 42 raw Elo points (1182 vs. 1140), while in English (1045 vs. 1081) and Chinese (1045 vs. 1053) the baseline holds the higher raw rating within the same statistical tie.
  Together, these results suggest language-dependent diminishing returns from elaborate multi-stage prompt engineering and agentic scaffolding once a strong frontier model is in the loop.

### [93] [Adaptive Filtering of the KV Cache: Diagnosing and Correcting Structural-Role Bias in LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13205)
*Soumil Mandal*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文分析了基于注意力的KV缓存淘汰机制（如H2O等）在长上下文模型中的表现，发现传统方法在结构化输入中会导致信号质量劣化并大幅降低准确率，提出了一种无需重训练、基于角色条件分配的新方法，有效缓解了这一问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长上下文模型受限于KV缓存大小，现有通过注意力累积分数选择保留Token的方法常常在结构化数据中引入噪声，导致重要内容丢失，准确率骤降。作者旨在找到减少内容信息损失的办法。

Method: 作者分析了基于注意力的KV淘汰机制的累积分数在结构化数据（如JSON）中的异常表现，并设计了一个“角色条件分配”算法，通过线性探测器识别Token角色，在不重训练模型的情况下，动态分配不同类型Token的缓存比例。

Result: 新算法在低缓存预算（<20%）下恢复了63-98%的准确率损失，在高预算下能与全缓存性能相当甚至略优。实验用4种种子，部分情况下提升有统计学意义。

Conclusion: 无需模型重训练、超参数简单的新算法能明显提升结构化输入下的缓存利用效率并显著恢复精度，但对于精确达到解析器层级的下游任务表现还有提升空间。

Abstract: Attention-based KV cache eviction (H2O and its descendants) compresses the memory-constrained state of a long-context model by ranking tokens on accumulated attention mass, treated here as signal energy, and keeping the heaviest. On schema-dense input streams such as nested JSON, this score acts as a non-stationary filter that disproportionately retains noise: a non-content sink role (delimiters or whitespace) carries an order of magnitude more energy than any content role, and structural KEY tokens are over-retained at roughly 1.8x the rate of the answer-carrying VALUE tokens, collapsing exact-match accuracy from 88% to 0% at a 5% budget as the signal-to-noise ratio of the retained state degrades. A counterfactual experiment establishes that suppressing KEY tokens is the best deployable filter. Our retraining-free, role-conditional allocation over SnapKV's windowed score, governed by a single tuned hyperparameter, closes 63-98% of the H2O gap at sub-20% budgets and, at higher budgets, modestly matches or exceeds full-cache accuracy -- a small, seed-sensitive denoising effect (borderline significant at B=0.50; not distinguishable from zero at B=0.30 over four seeds). A 15 MB linear role probe supplies these labels at negligible inference cost, though matching parser-level downstream accuracy remains open.

### [94] [GSM-Plus-BN: A Perturbation-Based Benchmark for Bangla Mathematical Reasoning in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13248)
*Bidyarthi Paul,Nahida Jannat Mayouree,Md. Asif Karim,Sagar Chandra Nath,Swastika Kundu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究提出并公开了GSM-Plus-BN，这是首个系统性扰动的孟加拉语数学推理数据集，并用其评估多个主流开源大模型在孟加拉语数学推理上的表现，发现现有模型在该任务上表现仍落后于英文。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型的数学推理能力主要聚焦于高资源语言（如英语），导致对孟加拉语等弱资源语言的算法发展与公平部署受限，同时缺乏系统性孟加拉语数学推理干扰数据集，无法评估模型鲁棒性及理解力。

Method: 从知名英文数学推理数据集GSM-Plus出发，通过人工翻译与扰动方法，构建了包含9,000条题目的孟加拉语数据集GSM-Plus-BN。采用标准提示和思维链提示两种方式，评测了6个主流开源大语言模型对这些数据的推理能力和鲁棒性。

Result: GPT-OSS-20B在标准提示下达到了96.08%的原始题准确率；但在多种扰动下，参数更大的Llama-3.3-70B与GPT-OSS-120B展现出更好的鲁棒性。整体而言，思维链提示较标准提示能明显提升大部分模型的推理水平，但所有模型在孟加拉语扰动数据上的表现仍显著低于其在英语上的表现。

Conclusion: GSM-PLUS-BN为孟加拉语数学推理研究提供了重要的基线和资源，同时实验证明当前主流模型在低资源语言扰动场景下表现不佳，需针对性改进算法以提升其公平性与鲁棒性。

Abstract: The evaluation of mathematical reasoning in large language models (LLMs) has predominantly focused on high-resource languages like English. This has created a significant barrier to the equitable development and deployment of AI in linguistically diverse regions such as Bangladesh, where over 230 million people speak Bengali. Despite this global significance, there has been minimal prior work on mathematical reasoning in Bengali and no existing research that systematically benchmarks a perturbated Bengali mathematical dataset, leaving a critical void in assessing model robustness and true comprehension beyond pattern recognition. This study addresses this gap by introducing GSM-Plus-BN, a novel perturbated Bengali mathematical dataset derived from the English GSM-Plus benchmark and verified by human translators. We evaluate six open-source LLMs Qwen3-32B, Llama-3.1-8B-Instant, Llama-3.3-70B-Versatile, Llama-4-Scout-17B-16E-Instruct, GPT-OSS-120B, and GPT-OSS-20B using a benchmark of 9,000 evaluation samples comprising 1,000 seed questions and 8,000 perturbed variants under both Standard Prompting and Chain-of-Thought (CoT) Prompting. Experimental results show that GPT-OSS-20B achieves the highest seed question accuracy of 96.08% under Standard Prompting, while larger models such as Llama-3.3-70B and GPT-OSS-120B demonstrate superior robustness across perturbation types. Furthermore, CoT prompting substantially improves reasoning for most models compared to Standard Prompting, yet a notable performance gap persists across all models relative to their English benchmarks, underscoring the inherent difficulty of perturbed Bengali text. This research makes a foundational contribution by providing GSM-PLUS-BN as a new resource and baseline for future Bengali mathematical reasoning research.

*Stylianos Loukas Vasileiou,Olga Derendiaeva*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 政策文件在治理中至关重要，但其论证方式常常隐晦，参与性承诺与管理性控制等相互矛盾的立场常共存，却很少被直接点明，主流计算方法又难以揭示其框架间复杂关系。

Method: 作者提出Apaf，一个LLM-符号混合流程，先利用LLM将政策文本中的论点分为协商性或管理性框架，再运用确定性规则结合LLM特征，自动提取四类框架介导的关系（能力削减、议程转移、工具性支持、规范性支持），最终形成可解释的争论结构图。

Abstract: Policy documents shape governance outcomes, but their reasoning is often implicit. Participatory commitments and managerial control routinely coexist in the same text, and the tensions between them are rarely stated directly. Existing computational approaches to policy discourse cannot express the frame-mediated relations that drive these tensions, where one argument narrows or instrumentalizes another rather than rejecting it. End-to-end summarization by large language models produces fluent text but offers little structure that domain experts can inspect or contest. We present Apaf, a hybrid LLM--symbolic pipeline that operationalizes critical discourse analysis as a quantitative bipolar argumentation framework over policy text. Arguments are first classified into deliberative or managerial frames. Four frame-mediated relation subtypes (agency reduction, agenda shift, instrumental support, and normative support) are then produced by deterministic rules over LLM-extracted features. We release a novel dataset of 100 sub-documents of disaster-risk-reduction policy from the USA, UK, Canada, and Australia, and show that the resulting argument graphs are accurate, interpretable, and stable across jurisdictions.

### [96] [Finding the Right Tables and Columns: A Benchmark and Corpus-Adaptive Embeddings for SQL Schema Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13311)
*Qingcheng Zeng,Puxuan Yu,Aman Mehta,Fuheng Zhao,Rajhans Samdani*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文关注于大规模SQL数据库中的模式(schema)检索，而非传统的SQL查询匹配，提出并系统评测了表和列级别的检索任务，并通过fine-tuning显著提升了预训练模型在该任务中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在实际大型数据库场景下，SQL检索任务首先需要从成千上万的表与列中找出相关结构（schema），而不是直接生成SQL语句。现有模型及评估多忽视这一关键步骤，影响了模型对实际企业级应用的适应性。

Method: 论文将5个主流text-to-SQL数据集重新构建为表/列级别的检索任务，比较了两种schema文档表示方式，并测试了现有文本与代码嵌入模型的效果。随后提出了corpus-adaptive fine-tuning方法：对目标schema库合成自然语言查询，挖掘粒度感知的难负样本，用对比损失微调305M嵌入模型。

Result: 微调后的305M模型recall@10从60.4提升到75.6，nDCG@10从51.9提升到68.0，性能超过了体量更大的4-8B嵌入模型，且同一技术也能提升8B模型到最优水平。离群数据集实验和泄漏审计进一步验证了能力的泛化性和可迁移性。

Conclusion: 论文确立了schema检索为独立的检索任务，提出无需人工标注、轻量级的模型自适应策略，在企业级大规模部署上具有实际指导意义。

Abstract: Retrieval in the SQL setting has largely been studied as the task of finding, within a large collection of SQL statements, the statement that answers a natural-language question. At scale, however, a more fundamental retrieval problem precedes generation: schema retrieval, identifying the tables and columns a question requires in a database that may contain thousands of them, far more than fit in a model's context. We argue that this step warrants first-class evaluation. To this end, we recast five text-to-SQL datasets (Spider, BIRD, BEAVER, and two LiveSQLBench variants) as retrieval tasks at both table and column granularity, covering realistic and enterprise-scale schemas under two document representations, and we show that off-the-shelf text and code embedders transfer poorly to this setting. We then propose corpus-adaptive fine-tuning: natural-language queries are synthesized directly from the target schema corpus, granularity-aware hard negatives are mined, and a 305M-parameter embedder is fine-tuned contrastively. This procedure raises average recall@10 from 60.4 to 75.6 (nDCG@10 from 51.9 to 68.0), making the 305M model the strongest retriever under one billion parameters and competitive with state-of-the-art embedders of 4-8B parameters, more than an order of magnitude larger. The same recipe improves an 8B state-of-the-art embedder from 77.8 to 78.4 recall@10, matching the best result on the benchmark and indicating that the adaptation is backbone-agnostic. Leave-one-corpus-out experiments and a leakage audit show that these gains reflect a transferable schema-retrieval ability rather than memorization of the evaluation data. Our results establish schema linking as a standalone retrieval task and lightweight, label-free corpus adaptation as a practical route to deploying it at enterprise scale.

</details>


### [97] [Meta-Learning Preferences for Multilingual LLM Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13315)
*Jiaying Lin,Seongho Son,Nam Phuong Tran,Long Tran-thanh,Ilija Bogunovic,Debmalya Mandal*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种元学习框架，通过利用多语言的人类反馈数据，提高低资源语言大语言模型对齐效率和效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现今大语言模型需要进行人类偏好对齐，但很多低资源语言缺乏足够的偏好数据，这导致多语种场景中的对齐效果不足。因此需要研究如何借助高资源语言已有的数据改善低资源语言模型的对齐能力。

Method: 提出了元学习（meta-learning）框架，结合了基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）和直接偏好优化（Direct Preference Optimization），利用其它语言的偏好数据获得可迁移的初始化参数。在目标低资源语言上使用极少量数据即可有效适应，并提供理论证明和实验证明。

Result: 在只有100条目标语言偏好样本的极低资源情况下，方法在多语基准测试上比基线最高提升28%的胜率，在不同目标语种与模型规模下均超越基线，且优势在不同训练语言组合与语言距离设定下依然维持。

Conclusion: 所提元学习方法可以极大改善低资源语言模型对齐问题，具备良好的跨语言迁移能力和实际应用潜力。

Abstract: Unequal availability of human preference data across languages poses a significant challenge for aligning large language models in multilingual settings. To address the lack of sufficient data in low-resource language alignment, we propose a meta-learning framework for Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback and Direct Preference Optimization. By leveraging preference data from other languages, our framework learns a transferable initialization that enables effective adaptation to a target language with minimal data. We provide theoretical guarantees for both the meta-reward modeling and meta-policy optimization settings, and empirically demonstrate the effectiveness of our approach on multilingual benchmarks. In an extremely low-resource setting with only 100 target-language preference samples, our approach achieves up to $28\%$ win-rate improvements over baseline methods, and consistently outperforms baselines across multiple target languages and model scales. Our approaches retain these advantages across different combinations of meta-training languages and varying linguistic distances from the target languages.

</details>


### [98] [Evaluation Ability Does Not Imply Optimization Utility: LLM-as-a-Judge Signals in Closed-Loop Table Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13347)
*Donghwan Kim*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文探讨了将大语言模型（LLM）作为“裁判”（judge）的有效性，特别是在表格识别任务上的回生（regeneration）环中。研究发现，当前LLM的裁判反馈信号较弱，选优效果有限，并不能显著优于随机选择，且存在结构保持失败等问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然LLM被广泛用作任务自动回生流程的反馈信号源（如在表格识别任务自动微调、优化等），但其作为评判者的有效性和利用价值尚未被充分实证或验证。作者希望通过有可控评价标准的表格识别任务体系，系统性地分析LLM-As-a-Judge这一方案的能力、局限和适用性。

Method: 作者选取了表格识别任务作为研究对象，利用FinTabNet与OmniDocBench数据集，并选用TEDS等确定性指标作为基线标准。通过在有无“结构保持”指令、不同judge反馈、不同迭代策略的控制实验下，比较LLM打分与最优方案之间的差异，并分析其表现。

Result: (1) LLM裁判信号弱、打分经常出现并列，排名不可复现，部分选优策略虽稍好于随机但优势来源复杂。(2) 就算没有具体裁判反馈，也会产生严重错误，且仅靠结构保持指令可显著降低严重错误率。(3) 结构保持指令虽然减轻了严重丢分，但整体性能未有提升。保持judge反馈时，结构保护效应也不稳定。

Conclusion: LLM作为评判者具有评价价值，但仅靠其打分难以完成有效的优化引导。实现迭代优化至少需要能确定性检测结构变动的准确度量信号，仅靠judge分数是不够的。

Abstract: LLM-as-a-judge is widely used to provide feedback and selection signals in closedloop regeneration, but this use remains insufficiently validated. We study it in table recognition, where deterministic TEDS evaluation provides a controlled testbed, using FinTabNet and OmniDocBench. Three findings emerge. First, judge signals were weak on both datasets: scores frequently tied, rankings were not reproducible, and the only selection policy that beat random on both datasets depended on an earliest-iteration tie rule, so its advantage cannot be attributed to the judge scores alone. Iteration produced better candidates, but the judge failed to recover them. Second, severe losses occurred even without specific judge feedback. A structurepreserving instruction significantly reduced the severe-loss rate on FinTabNet and was directionally consistent on OmniDocBench. The contrasts support target-preservation failure under unconstrained regeneration as a proximate mechanism of the observed severe losses. Third, the structure-preservation constraint reduced the severe-loss tail but produced no improvement. In an exploratory 2x2 analysis, the same protection was not stably observed when judge feedback was retained. These results do not dispute the value of LLMs as evaluators. Instead, they show that evaluation ability does not imply optimization utility. Iterative refinement requires, at minimum, a verification signal that deterministically detects structural change, rather than judge scores alone.

</details>


### [99] [A POS Tier Is the Key to Automated Annotation for Low-Resource Language Documentation: Neural Interlinear Glossing for Irabu, a Southern Ryukyuan Language](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13372)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手工对口语语料进行逐分词、多层注释极为耗时，尤其对濒危语言，专家与母语者资源紧缺下，自动化流程有助于加速语言文献抢救。

Result: 加入词性注释可使词汇注释大幅提升准确度，数据越稀少提升越明显（最多+11.6点准确率），且所需数据量减半。但自动词性标注若精度不高则会反而误导注释模型；当标注准确率超过88%后，增益才逐渐显现。

Abstract: Discourse data are the primary empirical basis of grammar writing in field linguistics, but producing interlinearized text is notoriously expensive - on the order of one hour of work per minute of recording. We implement a full neural annotation pipeline (morpheme segmentation, POS tagging, glossing) for Irabu Ryukyuan using deliberately small, transparent BiLSTM-CRF models, and evaluate it under a realistic hard constraint: approximately one hour of fully annotated discourse as the entire supervised resource. Two factors of the annotation itself are manipulated: its richness (with or without a POS tier) and its quantity (training budgets from 6 to 47 minutes). Gold POS improves grammatical glossing by +4.4 (SD 0.7) points (significant in all 5 seeds), and the gain grows as data shrink (+11.6 points at a quarter of the data); a POS tier more than halves the amount of glossed data needed to reach a given accuracy. In a fully automatic pipeline this gain is not yet realized: the tagger still errs on 12% of morphemes, and an incorrect POS misleads the glossing model more than no POS at all. The value is latent rather than lost: degrading gold POS with controlled noise shows the gain returning as tagger accuracy rises, with break-even near our tagger's current 88% and +1.6 to +3.2 points recovered at 92-96%. We conclude with a concrete recommendation for documentation practice: annotate quadrilinearly - text, POS, gloss, translation.

### [100] [GFlowRL: Scaling Distribution-Matching RL to Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13394)
*Xiaodong Liu,Michael Xu,Jack W. Stokes,Paul Smolensky,Doug Burger,Jianfeng Gao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新型的GFlowNet风格强化学习算法GFlowRL，能够去除在大模型中作为规范化因子的分区函数网络，简化工程结构、提升稳定性，并在数学、代码、对抗鲁棒性等多项任务上优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GFlowNet方法在匹配奖励分布、促进推理多样性方面表现出色，但难以扩展到大型模型和现代后训练流水线，分区函数网络反而成为梯度不稳定和工程负担的源头。

Method: 作者通过系统分析发现分区函数可被同批次Monte Carlo估计所替代，据此提出无需辅助分区网络的GFlowRL，同时引入重要性采样校正和非对称残差裁剪作为稳定器，保持奖励分布匹配目标。

Result: GFlowRL在数学、代码及对抗红队等任务上均超越现有类似方法，在Codeforces 14B模型规模下得分2048，AdvBench和HarmBench上ASR@1均为最高，并且可以无障碍迁移至最大235B参数的MoE配置，而对比方法FlowRL无法收敛。

Conclusion: GFlowRL是首个能横跨稠密及稀疏架构稳定扩展的GFlowNet风格强化学习算法，显著提升了方法可扩展性、稳定性和实用性。

Abstract: Generative Flow Networks (GFlowNets) offer a promising alternative to reward-maximizing reinforcement learning (RL) for large reasoning models, encouraging diverse reasoning paths by matching reward distributions rather than collapsing to dominant modes. Recent work shows promise on math and code, but scaling GFlowNet-style RL to modern post-training pipelines remains difficult: as model size, rollout horizon, reward noise, and distributed-systems complexity grow together, a learned prompt-conditional partition function becomes a source of gradient instability and engineering overhead rather than a useful normalizer. Through systematic analysis, we find that the learned partition function, previously treated as essential, can be replaced by an in-batch Monte Carlo estimate computed from the rollout group already required for training. We propose GFlowRL, a streamlined GFlowNet-style RL algorithm that removes the auxiliary partition network entirely while preserving the reward-distribution-matching objective, completed by two stabilizers: importance-sampling correction for rollout/trainer drift and asymmetric flow-gap clipping for outlier residuals. GFlowRL exceeds all counterparts on math, code, and adversarial red-teaming benchmarks, reaching a Codeforces rating of 2048 at the 14B scale (within 25 Elo of o3-mini) and attaining the highest average ASR@1 on AdvBench and HarmBench, outperforming the previous SOTA multi-turn attacker in a regime where FlowRL, a prior GFlowNet-style method, diverges. The same recipe transfers to all evaluated MoE configurations up to 235B parameters, where FlowRL again fails to converge. To our knowledge, GFlowRL is the first GFlowNet-style RL algorithm to scale stably across both dense and sparse architectures. Code will be at: https://github.com/microsoft/gflowrl

</details>


### [101] [Demystifying On-Policy Distillation: Roles, Pathologies, and Regulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13399)
*Rui Wang,Hongru Wang,Yi Chen,Boyang Xue,Tianqing Fang,Wenhao Yu,Kam-Fai Wong*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文系统性研究了大模型领域中在策略蒸馏（OPD）的机制及其潜在问题，提出信号调节方法提升效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管OPD已成为大模型后训练的重要方式，但其训练机制和潜在问题尚未被深入理解，有必要进行系统性的剖析，为后续优化提供理论和实践基础。

Method: 作者通过理论分析和大量实验，揭示OPD主要通过密集的token级别信号引导学生模型探索正确的推理路径，但其有效性严重依赖于引导信号质量。文中还分析了两类失效模式：学生-老师分布不匹配导致错误探索，以及token目标聚合引发的长度投机问题。提出优势截断和对数尺度压缩等轻量信号调节方法应对上述问题。

Result: 在七项基准任务上实验表明，提出的信号调节措施能有效缓和长度投机并提升知识蒸馏效果，超越其它OPD变种和RLVR基线方法。

Conclusion: 研究证明信号质量和调节手段远比单纯增大教师模型规模更关键，是确保OPD探索有效性的核心，相关调节方法值得后续应用和推广。

Abstract: On-policy distillation (OPD) has become a key paradigm in LLM post-training, yet its training dynamics remain poorly understood. We present a systematic study examining the role, pathologies, and regulations of OPD. We first clarify the role of OPD as an exploration catalyst: it steers the student toward correct reasoning paths via dense token-level guidance, without expanding capability ceiling. We confirm this by showing that prompt diversity matters more than per-problem sampling numbers, and critically, that the effectiveness of OPD hinges entirely on the quality of its guiding signal. This dependency exposes two pathologies that derail exploration. The Student-Teacher Mismatch occurs when a large teacher-student distributional gap causes the guiding signal to misalign with task correctness, steering exploration in counterproductive directions. Length Exploitation arises when the aggregated token-level objective creates length-dependent shortcuts, allowing the student to game the reward landscape through response truncation or redundant padding, exploring degenerate length modes rather than reasoning strategies. To tame these pathologies, we investigate lightweight signal regulations: advantage clipping and log-scale compression, ensuring exploration is guided by faithful signals. Experiments across seven benchmarks demonstrate that these regulations alleviate length exploitation and enable effective distillation, stably surpassing OPD variants and RLVR baselines, thereby confirming that well-regulated signal quality, rather than mere teacher scale, governs successful exploration in OPD.

  <summary>Details</summary>

We formalize the task as predicting, at every time t, a pair (shabad_id, line_idx) or null, and organize the problem space into a 2x2 matrix along two orthogonal axes: live vs. offline (causal vs. full-audio access) and blind vs. oracle (shabad identity discovered vs. given). We release v1 of the benchmark - 4 hand-annotated Kirtan recordings x 3 cold-start offsets = 12 evaluation cases, ~57 minutes of scored audio - together with a scorer that computes frame accuracy at 1s resolution over a scored region, with a 1s collar and gap-tolerant scoring at segment boundaries. We describe a reference system (fine-tuned 120M IndicConformer -> fuzzy matcher -> state machine; INT8 ONNX; RTF ~0.05 on one Apple Silicon core) that achieves 57.9% overall frame accuracy across all 12 cases (10/12 correct shabad locks) on the hardest variant (live x blind). We compare against three trivial baselines (empty, shifted-5s, perfect) and discuss why standard ASR metrics (WER/CER) measure transcription accuracy rather than the display accuracy this task requires. The benchmark, reference system, and a live deployment are released under permissive licenses to facilitate further improvements.

We introduce DevicesWorld, a large-scale executable benchmark for cross-device collaborative operation. DevicesWorld contains 6,140 tasks and integrates three classes of device environments -- mobile, desktop, and IoT -- into a unified cross-device interaction and evaluation framework. Abstract: We describe our BioASQ Task 14B 2026 system. Retrieval unions two parallel pipelines - a hybrid first stage (dense BGE + BM25 + RRF, reaching R@200 = 99.3% on the BioASQ-13b historical archive) and an agent-driven pipeline that decomposes the question over PubMed, Europe PMC, and iCite - with a BGE cross-encoder quality gate flagging weakly-supported questions for selective re-retrieval. On Task 12B 2024 validation, a cost-pragmatic re-retrieval policy beats a skill-strict baseline significantly on list F1 and list precision, at 12% lower re-retrieval cost. Holding prompt and model fixed across val and test 13B (different question sets), list F1 rises by +0.132 absolute on the BioASQ-released gold-input pool, consistent with substantial retrieval-side headroom. For Phase B answering we decompose multi-model ensemble lift into a selection component bounded by the per-question oracle and a fusion component that aggregators can exceed. The decomposition predicts before any experiment that LLM-as-judge wins on selection-dominated metrics (yes/no, multi-reference ROUGE) but is structurally insufficient on the recall component of fusion-friendly metrics (factoid rank-1, list recall). On Task 13B 2025 our synonym-union resolver wins list recall on every head, while GPT-5.5 solo retains the list-F1 lead because the resolver's wider item set costs precision. On the Task 14B 2026 preliminary leaderboard our team places first on the combined-exact aggregate on three of the eight (phase x batch) leaderboards, wins four individual question-type cells, and takes #1 on Phase B b3 ideal.

</details>


### [108] [Graded Entity-Familiarity Readouts in Language Models: Polish Adaptation, Cross-Language Robustness, and Refusal Steering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13568)
*Grzegorz Brzezinka*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文探讨了大语言模型（LLM）在生成答案前，是否能估计自己对实体的熟悉程度。作者利用波兰语数据和多模型分析，发现通过最后输入Token的激活可以有效区分真实与伪造实体，还能一定程度反映实体流行度。熟悉度探针对不同输入语种有较好鲁棒性，对模型拒答行为有显著影响，并作为生成前的过滤机制表现良好。行为层面的出错预测仍需结合生成后检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型有时会在知识受限时产生错误，尤其在遇到陌生实体。这一研究旨在判断LLM是否能够在生成答案之前自我评估对特定实体的知识熟悉度，从而指导模型何时选择“拒答”或生成答案，提高模型可靠性和安全性。

Method: 作者选择了12个不同的指令微调模型（覆盖Bielik、PLLuM、Gemma-4和Qwen3等），利用包含1,440个波兰实体及部分伪造实体的新数据集，对各模型最后输入Token的激活值进行统计与建模，设计“熟悉度探针”。分析探针输出与实体流行度（Wikipedia浏览量）相关性，并测试输入语言变化（波兰语vs.英语）的影响。还探讨对模型拒答策略的干预与生成前后过滤机制的有效性。

Result: 所有模型的熟悉度探针都能区分真实和伪造实体。在波兰本地化模型（Bielik/PLLuM）中，熟悉度探针分数还能较强地反映实体流行度，与参数量无关。输入语言切换影响较小。对Gemma-4-12B模型，调整探针方向后，对熟悉或陌生实体的拒答率可精确控制。熟悉度探针作为生成前过滤机制与其他方法具有竞争力，但生成后的检测对于行为预测更有效。

Conclusion: LLM在生成前能够通过内部表示对实体熟悉度进行分级估计，这一能力既与本地化有关也部分独立于参数规模。熟悉度探针可为拒答机制和知识边界自识别提供技术基础，但与行为决策（如拒答）之间有分离。融合熟悉度与其他机制，有望提升模型可靠性与安全性。

Abstract: Can a language model estimate its familiarity with an entity before generating an answer? We study activations at the final prompt token in twelve instruction-tuned models from the Bielik, PLLuM, Gemma-4, and Qwen3 families, using a new dataset of 1,440 Polish entities spanning four domains and ten Wikipedia-pageview deciles, plus fabricated controls. Familiarity-probe scores separate real from fabricated entities in every family; in the Polish-adapted Bielik and PLLuM families they additionally track entity popularity (model-mean Spearman $ρ$ 0.28-0.57, versus at most 0.11 in Gemma-4 and Qwen3), a pattern more strongly associated with Polish adaptation than with parameter count in this model sample. In a paired experiment on two families, probes retain 96-101% of within-language AUROC when the Polish question stem is replaced with an English one around unchanged entity names, showing robustness to prompt language in this setting. In Gemma-4-12B, the only model that natively refuses, adding a one-dimensional familiarity direction at a single layer moves refusal rates monotonically in both directions (0.24 to 1.00 on well-known entities; 0.73 to 0.00 on unknown ones). Finally, a calibrated familiarity probe is competitive among pre-generation abstention gates, although post-generation detectors better predict behavioral error on average. These results support a graded pre-generation entity-familiarity readout, and a separation between representational familiarity and the policy that converts it into abstention.

### [109] [Memory as a Controlled Process: Learned Adaptive Memory Management for LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13591)
*Eric Hanchen Jiang,Zhi Zhang,Yuchen Wu,Levina Li,Dong Liu,Xiao Liang,Rui Sun,Yubei Li,Edward Sun,Haozheng Luo,Zhaolu Kang,Aylin Caliskan,Kai-Wei Chang,Ying Nian Wu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新型的LLM智能体记忆管理框架MemCon，能自适应地优化如何访问和管理外部记忆系统，在多个基准测试中提升任务表现并减少资源消耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体通过固定启发式规则访问外部记忆，但这种静态机制无法适应任务不同阶段或上下文的需求，限制了智能体的学习和表现。动态、高效并能自我调节的记忆管理机制成为提升能力的关键。

Method: 作者将记忆操作建模为马尔可夫决策过程（MDP），通过在线学习策略，决定何时、检索什么、检索多少，以及何时融合或遗忘记忆。框架适用于任何记忆实现，无需预训练和额外LLM请求，通过轻量级表格型上下文赌博器结合UCB探索快速收敛。

Result: 在6个基准测试、3种智能体框架和3种LLM骨干上，MemCon在任务成功率上相较多种记忆基线最高提升15.2个百分点，并能减少5-20%的Token消耗。

Conclusion: MemCon具备良好的通用性和高效的自适应能力，在广泛场景中显著优化了LLM智能体的任务表现和资源利用效率，为外部记忆管理提供了新的发展方向。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) agents increasingly rely on external memory systems to accumulate experience across tasks. Yet nearly all existing approaches, from graph-structured memories to reflective insight stores, access memory through fixed, hand-designed heuristics. We argue that this static view of memory is a core bottleneck for agentic learning because optimal memory behavior is fundamentally context-dependent. The early stages of the tasks, benefit from minimal retrieval because memory is sparse; recurring goal types benefit from plan reuse rather than generic nearest-neighbor lookup; stuck agents benefit from re-retrieval with alternative queries; and across long task streams, the memory store itself must be consolidated and pruned to remain useful. We present Memory as a Controlled Process (MemCon), a framework that models memory operations as a Markov Decision Process and learns an online policy that adaptively decides when, what, and how much to retrieve, when to inject a distilled plan, and when to consolidate or forget. MemCon is backend-agnostic: it wraps any existing memory implementation, learns from task-by-task binary feedback with no pretraining and no additional LLM calls, and uses a lightweight tabular contextual bandit with UCB exploration that converges within tens of tasks. Across 6 benchmarks, 3 agent frameworks, and 3 LLM backbones, MemCon consistently outperforms multiple memory baselines by up to 15.2 points in task success while reducing token consumption by 5--20%.

### [110] [Analogical Deep Research: Retrieving and Integrating Historical Analogies for Foresight Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13602)
*Yongqiang Chen,Guangyi Chen,Yuewen Sun,Kun Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了类比深度研究（ADR）任务，并创造了相应基准（ADR-bench），用于评估大型语言模型（LLM）代理在前景分析中寻找和利用历史类比的能力。研究发现现有LLM代理在寻找类比时更关注表面特征，难以识别深层机制。针对该难题，作者提出并实现了因果类比研究者（CANA）框架，有效提升了类比生成能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Systematic comparisons between current situations and structurally similar past events in the historical, i.e., historical analogies, is among the most powerful tools for foresight analysis. In this work, we present a new task called Analogical Deep Research (ADR) to Large Language Model (LLM) agents and construct the first ADR benchmark ADR-bench to study whether LLM agents are able to find and leverage historical analogies when doing foresight analysis. Our investigation reveals a key obstacle: LLM agents are poor at finding analogies because they match on surface features rather than underlying mechanisms. We argue that ADR is inherently a causal question as it requires understanding why the event occurred. Based on our theoretical analysis, we propose two principles required for ADR, including the mechanism alignment and cross-analogy confirmation. Built upon our theoretical results, we propose a new agentic framework called Causal Analogical Researcher (CANA) that guides LLMs to find and integrate historical analogies. CANA incorporates a simple yet effective structural decomposition representation, and integrates structural feedback for reflective improvements of historical analogy identification and integration. We show that CANA brings up to 10% improvements in historical analogy generation, and surpasses the state-of-the-art deep research agents in the ADR-bench. Case studies with the ongoing events confirm the effectiveness of CANA in leveraging historical analogies.

### [111] [Self-Evolving Agent Harnesses via Gated Semantic Quality-Diversity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13683)
*Xiaotian Luo,Fengxingyu Wang,Chuanrui Hu,Dizhan Xue,Yafeng Deng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种LLM agent自进化的外部系统（harness）优化框架，通过分离改进建议与有效性验证，使性能提升更可控、可信，并验证了其在多个领域的大幅泛化提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在实际部署中，LLM模型常被冻结，无法微调权重，工程师可以操作的主要是外部harness（如提示、知识注入等）。但如何科学地评估harness改动带来的真实贡献，避免过拟合和测量噪声，一直是难题。论文致力于自动、可靠地优化harness，提高实际应用性能。

Method: 框架将“提出修改（patch）”与“评估是否有效”分开：LLM负责检测失败点并生成补丁建议，所有采样与显著性评估交由确定性代码处理，从而确保被‘采纳’的补丁可信。提出抗过拟合的归档策略，将补丁按其解决的“病理点（问题x原因）”而非对应task存档，并用密封测试集最终检验泛化。

Result: 在7个领域/任务上，使用此自进化harness方法，对固定参数的开源大模型进行优化后，在密封测试集上获得了9至15.5个百分点的准确率提升，并且86-147%的训练集提升被保留，显示方法带来的性能改进具有较强的泛化性。

Conclusion: harness通过自动诊断与有效性严格验证，可实现显著且可靠的性能提升；更重要的是，成效并不依赖具体补丁或模型家族，而是依赖“诊断-归因-信用”循环机制，因此该方法具有良好的迁移性和广泛适用性。

Abstract: An LLM agent's real-task performance is shaped as much by the harness around its model as by the frozen model itself: its prompts, injected knowledge, runtime control, and configuration. In deployment the harness is often the only lever available, so improving it automatically is the natural way to raise performance without touching the weights. The hard part is not generating changes but knowing which one truly helped. Self-generated feedback is noisy, and an apparent gain can be a measurement artifact or an edit that merely overfits the tasks it was tuned on. We present a self-evolving agent-harness framework that separates proposing changes from crediting them: a language model diagnoses failures and proposes patches, while all sampling, measurement, and significance testing are owned by deterministic code, so every credited improvement is trustworthy by construction. Patches populate a gated, categorical quality-diversity archive (GSME) keyed on the (WHERE x WHY) pathology an edit addresses rather than the tasks it fixes, an anti-overfitting inductive bias; generalization is measured on a sealed test scored only after evolution. Across seven domains with a frozen open-weight model, the harness is train-selected and scored once on a sealed test; its credited gains there are +9 to +15.5pp and retain 86-147% of the training gain, evidence they generalize rather than overfit. The winning patch tracks the model's dominant pathology, not its size or family: changing the model can change the pathology and the patch, while the same pathology-to-patch match recurs across two model families. What transfers is the diagnose-and-credit loop, not any specific harness.

### [112] [The Test Oracle Problem in Synthetic LLM-as-Judge Corpora: Disappearance, Distortion and a Validation Protocol](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13707)
*Serkan Ballı*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文揭示了将大型语言模型（LLM）生成内容用于判断（LLM-as-judge）系统的偏差分析时，若生成步骤出现隐蔽的结构性故障，将导致严重但难以察觉的实验偏差。只有通过人工阅读可察觉这些问题，聚合性统计指标无法发现。作者提出了一种改进的验证流程，以增强该类研究的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM-as-judge体系在评估偏差时，经常用LLM自身生成的答案作为“负样本”。但这类方法隐藏风险，尤其是生成过程出现意外故障时，偏差分析结果会被严重扭曲，却难以被自动化手段发现。

Method: 作者分析了一个多语言（英-土双语）‘忠实性评判语料库’，发现因为判别和生成步骤共用解码预算，导致生成答案极度简短,严重影响评判。通过再现实验、原理解释、受控实验等方式，系统揭示了故障的产生过程及影响，并对比了两类负样本构建方法的健壮性。

Result: 发现因参数共享导致的故障使得判别准确率大幅下降32个百分点，且这一影响通过不同样本规模（N=50至N=500）均能复现。进一步发现手工扰动（deterministic perturbation）构建的负样本则可以通过自动比对，无成本捕捉同类故障。

Conclusion: 构建基于LLM生成的语料时，负样本存在无法机制性核查的脆弱性。作者建议采用手工扰动产生负样本，或在完全自动化时引入严格的人工验证流程，以避免因生成异常带来的评估失真。

Abstract: Studies of bias in LLM-as-judge systems typically build synthetic corpora by prompting an LLM to generate a hallucinated answer to pair with a factual one, then presenting both to a judge. We report a case in which this generation step silently failed, and use it to argue that the failure mode is structural rather than incidental. In a multilingual (Turkish/English) faithfulness-judgment corpus, a decoding-budget parameter shared between judging and generation calls truncated one producer's hallucinated answers to a few words. The resulting items produced a large, statistically robust effect: a 32-point cross-lingual collapse in one judge's selection accuracy, replicated from N=50 to N=500, explained by a three-layer mechanistic account, and confirmed by a controlled producer-swap experiment, none of which was real. The effect vanished to ceiling once the shared parameter was corrected, and only manual reading of the raw generations, not any aggregate statistical check, exposed the fault. A second measured bias (Markdown-formatting preference) was not fabricated but distorted by the same fault, its magnitude and in one case its sign shifting with stimulus length, a mode aggregate metrics cannot distinguish from the first. We frame the underlying vulnerability using the test oracle problem: corpora whose negative examples are LLM-generated carry no mechanical way to verify item integrity, while corpora built by deterministic perturbation of a gold answer carry an item-level oracle for free. A positive control supports this claim directly: an analogous fault injected into a minimal perturbation-based corpus is caught with 100% accuracy by a zero-cost, zero-human gold-to-negative string comparison. We close with a validation protocol, derived from our own case, for analysts working in the oracle-less regime that we argue describes most contemporary multilingual LLM-as-judge corpora.

### [113] [Self-supervised Speech Comparison for L2 Phone, Rhythm, and Intonation Scoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13721)
*Stephen McIntosh,Reuben Smit,Daisuke Saito,Nobuaki Minematsu,Herman Kamper*

Main category: cs.CL

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的L2语音评估主要集中于音段（语音）层面，并且依赖人工标注的训练数据，导致难以在资源有限环境中大规模应用。同时，节奏和语调等超音段特征的评分尚未被充分研究。

Method: 利用自监督模型WavLM提取得到的语音表征，采用动态时间规整（DTW）算法，无需转写文本，直接比较L2学习者与母语者模板的语音。在音段评估上，直接进行DTW对齐评分；节奏方面，根据DTW对齐路径的变形程度开发了新的评分方法；语调方面，将韵律残差上的DTW距离与基频、强度等特征结合进行评估。

Result: 音段层面的DTW评分在人类一致性检测上超越了真人；节奏评分的新方法达到了接近或达到人类水平；语调评分虽有提升，但在某些任务上表现仍有限。

Abstract: L2 speech assessment has traditionally focused on phonetic assessment, leaving the scoring of suprasegmental features such as rhythm and intonation underexplored. Moreover, assessment methods often require training with labeled L2 speech data, making them difficult to apply in low-resource settings. We investigate whether DTW over self-supervised WavLM representations can provide a text-free framework for assessing phonetic accuracy, rhythm, and intonation in English and Japanese L2 speech. Results show that a basic DTW-based approach that compares learner speech to native templates exceeds human agreement on holistic and sentence-level phonetic scoring. For rhythm, we introduce methods that measure the degree of warping in the DTW alignment path; our best method approaches human-level performance. For intonation, we combine DTW distance over prosodic residuals with pitch and intensity features, but performance remains more modest on some tasks. Our results point to self-supervised representations as a promising, text-free basis for multi-aspect pronunciation assessment.

### [114] [Post-Training Shifts Confidence: A Three-Stage Analysis of How SFT, RL, and OPD Shape Pre-, Intra-, and Post-CoT Calibration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13753)
*Shuhao Li,Guodong Du,Anhao Zhao,Wanyu Lin,Tianyu Yuan,Xiaoyu Shen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出并分析了一种三阶段校准框架，系统评估大型语言模型（LLMs）在推理过程中的置信度演化，并提出了基于位置的置信度策略PosConf，显著提升了答案聚合和早停的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前对LLM的后训练方法（如监督微调、强化学习、依策略蒸馏）的评估通常只依赖最终答案的准确率，忽视了推理过程中置信度的表现和演变。本研究希望深入分析和优化这一过程，提升模型推理的可解释性和实用性。

Method: 提出“三阶段校准框架”，分别在推理前（难度估计）、推理中（早停）、推理后（答案聚合）评估置信度。对比分析三种主流后训练方法在每阶段的置信度表现，并设计了PosConf算法，仅采用置信度高、位置可靠的区间进行信息聚合。

Result: （1）OPD方法在推理前置信度最优，SFT在推理过程中适合早停，RL在答案聚合时最可靠；（2）RL置信度在路径确定后才有信息性，OPD置信度则早期有效但后期反校准；（3）PosConf策略可将RL聚合得分提升6.1分，OPD早停在紧凑token预算下提升最高4.3分。

Conclusion: 对LLM置信度的有效利用应当结合推理阶段和相对位置，分阶段、分位置灵活采纳置信信息，能进一步提升模型推理可靠性与实际效果。

Abstract: Large language models have made strong reasoning gains through supervised fine-tuning, reinforcement learning, and on-policy distillation, yet these post-training methods are usually evaluated only by final-answer accuracy. We study how they reshape confidence during reasoning. We introduce a three-stage calibration framework that evaluates confidence before, during, and after chain-of-thought generation, corresponding to difficulty estimation, early termination, and answer aggregation. Through a controlled comparison on mathematical reasoning benchmarks, we find that OPD provides the most useful pre-reasoning confidence, SFT gives the strongest online signal for early stopping, and RL produces the most reliable trace-level signal for aggregation. We further show that confidence reliability is position-dependent: RL confidence becomes informative after a path-commitment phase, while OPD confidence is useful early but can become inversely calibrated later. Based on this observation, we propose PosConf, a position-aware confidence strategy that uses confidence only from reliable relative-position intervals. PosConf improves RL answer aggregation by 6.1 points over majority voting and consistently improves OPD early stopping under tight token budgets, with gains up to 4.3 points by avoiding its later inverse-calibration region, showing that \emph{confidence in reasoning models should be used both stage-wise and position-awarely}. Our code is available at https://github.com/EIT-NLP/Post-Training-Calibration.

</details>


### [115] [SPyCE: Skill-Policy Co-evolution for Multimodal Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13854)
*Ru Zhang,Weijie Qiu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为SPyCE（Skill-Policy Co-evolution）的新框架，通过对多模态推理轨迹进行技能蒸馏与协同进化，显著提升多模态智能体的任务表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态智能体在任务执行中，RL方法只用奖励信号，无法有效提取和复用通用技能，而记忆法依赖静态回溯，不能动态进化技能库，难以提升泛化能力。亟需一种在训练期间不断进化、能与策略协同优化、并可复用的技能提取方法。

Method: 提出SPyCE框架，将轨迹分解为分层技能（局部执行技能与高阶流程技能），随着RL训练动态建立和进化技能库。训练时，策略模型检索并利用技能库指导决策，同时优秀的策略拓展技能库，形成闭环共进化。

Result: 在八项基准测试中，SPyCE均优于传统RL和记忆库方法。消融实验表明分层技能设计和技能-策略共进化机制对性能提升至关重要。

Conclusion: 联合技能-策略优化为构建高效多模态智能体提供了新范式，SPyCE框架显著增强了智能体的推理和泛化能力。

Abstract: Multimodal agents that think with images iteratively manipulate visual evidence and invoke tools across many steps. Existing reinforcement learning methods reduce trajectories to scalar rewards, forcing the policy to discover reusable tool-use patterns from scratch on every new task; memory-based alternatives retain past experience, yet they rely on test-time retrieval, without updating the policy to absorb reusable patterns from that experience. Our key insight is that multimodal reasoning trajectories should be distilled into reusable skills that co-evolve with the policy during training, rather than being consumed as rewards or retrieved from a static store. To this end, we propose SPyCE (Skill-Policy Co-evolution), a framework that distills trajectories into a hierarchical skill library and updates it throughout reinforcement learning. Execution skills capture local visual operations, while workflow skills encode high-level priors that orchestrate tool use. During training, the policy model conditions on retrieved skills to guide its rollouts, while the skill library evolves using valuable rollouts generated by the policy. This creates a closed loop in which improved policies yield better skills, and the evolving skill library, in turn, provides stronger priors for policy rollouts. Experiments across eight benchmarks demonstrate that SPyCE consistently outperforms both RL-based and memory-based baselines. Further analysis reveals that both the hierarchical skill design and the co-evolution mechanism are critical to our design. These results suggest joint skill-policy optimization as a promising paradigm for building capable multimodal agents.

</details>


### [116] [High-Order Question Generation in a Multilingual Educational Context](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13901)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高阶问题有助于批判性思维培养，但教师提问多为低阶，自动生成高阶问题困难，且现有研究大多局限于布鲁姆分类学，且多为英语环境，亟需探索多语言情境下的新方法。

Method: 采用两种替代性教学框架（Claim-Evidence-Reasoning和Divergent Questioning），在巴斯克语、西班牙语和英语中设计提示词，通过开源和专有大语言模型自动生成问题，并由教师评估这些问题的高阶属性。

Result: 无论是开源还是专有模型，都能较好地在三种语言中生成问题，但实际被教师认可为高阶的仅约占一半。采用新的框架可生成结构和概念更为多样的问题。

Conclusion: 替代性教育框架在多语言高阶问题生成上具有互补和可行性，可为布鲁姆分类学之外的问题构建提供新思路，但提升高阶问题比例仍需进一步探索。

Abstract: Critical thinking is a fundamental skill that helps learners move beyond simple memorization. One way to develop this skill is through high-order questioning. However, crafting such questions remains a challenge for educators, and classroom practices tend to rely on low-order questions. Large Language Models have demonstrated strong capabilities in generating high-order questions, especially when guided by prompts based on Bloom's Taxonomy. Yet, existing research has largely centered on this framework and focused only on English. This study addresses these gaps by introducing prompts grounded in two alternative frameworks: Claim-Evidence-Reasoning and Divergent Questioning within a multilingual context using Basque, Spanish, and English. Results indicate that while both an open-source and a proprietary model rather effectively generate questions in all three languages, only about half of the answerable questions are recognized by teachers as high-order. A positive finding is that the alternative frameworks produce structurally and conceptually varied questions, suggesting they could complement each other and provide viable alternatives to Bloom's Taxonomy.

### [117] [DeepStress: Stress-Testing Deep Search Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13920)
*Ismael Rousseau,Geraldine Damnati,Frederic Bechet*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了DeepStress框架，通过合成环境控制证据质量，对搜索智能体在面对低质量信息时的稳健性进行压力测试，并发现其处理不可靠信息的能力存在显著差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实应用中低质量证据可能导致搜索智能体严重失败，但相关研究和评测较少，因此需要开发可控的压力测试框架评估其鲁棒性。

Result: 测试结果显示，现有的搜索智能体在应对不可靠信息时能力差异显著。实验还引入了新指标以更好地评估系统性能及参数知识与外部检索知识之间的交互。

Abstract: While search agents demonstrate impressive capabilities in multi-step question answering, their robustness to poor-quality evidence remains under-explored. This phenomenon occurs rarely in realistic benchmarks but can lead to dramatic failure in real life applications. Therefore in this study we propose DeepStress, a stress testing framework that controls the frequency of challenging evidence by replacing the retrieval module of search agents with a controlled synthetic environment. We use this framework to control three dimensions that can affect document reliability: trustworthiness, relevance, and factuality. ### [118] [DeltaMerge-LowRes: Composing Language and Task Deltas for Low-Resource Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13967)
*Son Ha Xuan,Xuan-Bach Le,Phat T. Tran-Truong*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在低资源NLP场景下，将多语种编码器分别在语言和任务两个维度上独立适应，并在推理阶段通过不同规则在权重空间中组合的方法，显著提升了非洲语言多任务表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法通常需在新语言与新任务的组合上进行昂贵的联合微调，但实际低资源条件下难以获得足够标注样本，因此亟需更高效的语言与任务适应方式。

Method: 提出ΔMergeLowRes方法，分别从无标注单语文本学习语言delta（Δ_L），从有标签英文数据学习任务delta（Δ_T），再于推理时在权重空间用加法、激活引导、稀疏感知及创新的cross-axis TIES等四种组合规则合成最终模型。cross-axis TIES对TIES-Merging作了调整，使其适用于语言与任务轴。

Result: 在四类任务和四种非洲语言（158个实验单元）上，用10,000次bootstrap评估，cross-axis TIES至少有三种语言的摘要任务chrF提升4-7分，QA任务F1提升2.32，EM提升2.91，稀疏感知融合使分类任务的ECE降低36%。

Conclusion: 不同的组合规则显著影响模型在合并后对信息的保留、抑制与校准能力，cross-axis TIES在低资源跨语言多任务场景具备突出优势。所有实验细节已全部开源。

Abstract: Adapting a multilingual encoder to a new language \emph{and} a new task with only a few hundred gold examples is a common low-resource NLP setting, yet the two axes are usually fused via an expensive language--task fine-tuning run. We ask whether they can instead be trained separately and recombined in weight space. \DeltaMergeLowRes{} learns a language delta $Δ_L$ from unlabeled monolingual text and a task delta $Δ_T$ from labeled English data, then composes them at inference under one of four rules: additive, activation-guided, sparsity-aware, and a novel \emph{cross-axis TIES}. The new rule adapts the TIES-Merging steps of trimming, sign election, and merging to the language and task axes rather than to two task axes. Holding $(Δ_L,Δ_T)$ fixed across rules on four task families and four African languages ($158$ evaluated cells, $10{,}000$-sample paired bootstrap per cell), we find: (i) cross-axis TIES wins summarisation on $3/4$ languages by $+4$ to $+7$ chrF (chrF $18.59$ vs.\ $13.80$ task-only); (ii) it improves QA F1 by $+2.32$ and EM by $+2.91$; and (iii) sparsity-aware merging cuts classification ECE by $36\%$ at parity macro-F1. The composition rule materially changes what the merged model preserves, suppresses, and calibrates. We release all JSON traces and a claim ledger.

</details>


### [119] [Constraint-Aware Counterfactual Editing for Aspect-Based Sentiment Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13977)
*S M Rafiuddin,Vamsi Krishna Pavuluri,Atriya Sen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种新的生成和验证面向方面情感分析（ABSA）反事实样本的框架CAVE-ABSA，实现针对具体方面的情感翻转，同时保持其他方面和句子语义的完整性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的反事实生成方法更多关注整个句子的标签翻转，常常忽视了对具体方面的情感控制，导致生成内容往往存在方面无效、语义漂移或自相矛盾等问题，亟需一种能生成高质量方面级反事实样本的方法，推动ABSA模型鲁棒性研究。

Method: 提出CAVE-ABSA框架，包含四步：首先定位目标方面对应的主观表达；其次对相关片段进行受控反事实重写；然后通过修复模块优化初始生成；最后从方面有效性、语义相似性、结构一致性、编辑最小化、流畅性以及矛盾检测等维度筛选样本。

Result: CAVE-ABSA 能有效生成高质量、符合实际需求的方面级反事实样本，为ABSA模型的数据增强和鲁棒性评估提供了有力支持。

Conclusion: 通过生成和验证分离，CAVE-ABSA 能更加可靠地产生有意义的方面局部反事实样本，有助于检测和提升现有ABSA模型对方面相关情感推理的依赖程度。

Abstract: Aspect-Based Sentiment Analysis (ABSA) requires models to identify sentiment toward specific aspects rather than relying on the global polarity of a sentence. This makes counterfactual evaluation especially challenging: a valid counterfactual should flip the sentiment of one target aspect while preserving the sentiment of all non-target aspects, semantic meaning, fluency, and factual consistency. Existing counterfactual generation methods often focus on sentence-level label flipping and may produce edits that are fluent but aspect-invalid, semantically drifting, or contradictory. To address this limitation, we propose CAVE-ABSA, a Constraint-Aware Validated Editing framework for generating and validating aspect-level counterfactuals. CAVE-ABSA localizes the opinion span associated with the target aspect, performs controlled counterfactual rewriting, refines candidates through a repair module, and filters them using aspect-level verification, semantic similarity, AMR-guided structural preservation, edit minimality, fluency, and contradiction detection. The framework is designed to construct validated counterfactual ABSA datasets for robustness evaluation and data augmentation. By explicitly separating generation from validation, CAVE-ABSA provides a principled approach for producing meaningful aspect-local counterfactuals and for testing whether ABSA models truly rely on aspect-grounded sentiment reasoning.

</details>


### [120] [Can an Old Dog Be Taught New Tricks? Taking LLMs Beyond Sentence Level Translation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14040)
*Alaina Brandt*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种基于RAG的自动翻译系统PAT，可实现超越逐句翻译的文档级翻译，并结合了真实语料库以提升翻译的语篇与语用适应性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的自动翻译系统（包括CAT和MT）主要基于逐句翻译，难以适应跨语言的篇章结构和语用差异，尤其在英西翻译场景下，目标语言文本在结构和风格上往往需要重大调整，而传统方法很难实现。该论文旨在探索LLM能否通过引入上下文和用户定制规则，进行更接近人工的整体文本翻译。

Method: 作者提出了PAT系统，结合RAG框架，将用户设定的规范与美式英语和拉美西班牙语的长文本真实语料库进行匹配，并将段落、章节及文档级示例输入LLM以生成文档级译文。翻译效果通过自定义MQM评判标准，由具备专业背景的译者评估三项不同AI生成英文论文译成LATAM和墨西哥西班牙语的自动译文。六组自动译文基于不同提示与语料设置进行比较。

Result: 实验表明，简单提示未能实现实质性改革，结合用户规范和语料后，部分系统译文能显著进行语篇和风格重组，但效果不稳定。整体结果显示，LLM具备逐步摆脱逐句翻译惯性的潜力，但有效性和稳定性尚需改进。

Conclusion: LLM自动翻译系统可借助丰富上下文和语料，初步实现文档级重组与本地化，超越传统逐句翻译模式。但实现高质量自动“重述式”翻译仍有技术难题，有必要进一步完善系统设计、语料处理与评估体系。

Abstract: Automatic translation systems, from CAT tools to MT, overwhelmingly treat translation as a sentence-by-sentence act. This paper asks whether LLMs can be moved beyond that paradigm through whole-document, corpus-informed translation. We present PAT (Pragmatic Auto-Translator), a RAG-based system that pairs user-configured specifications with context from a comparable corpus of authentic longform texts in U.S. English and Latin American Spanish, passing retrieved paragraph-, section-, and document-level examples to an LLM for whole-document generation. The goal is draft translation for professional verification: target texts reformulated to fit their Spanish-language context, where discourse organization, rhetorical style, and pragmatic norms differ meaningfully from English. We evaluated six automatic translations of essays on generative AI across three projects using a customized MQM typology, assessed by two trained evaluators working from U.S. English into LATAM and Mexican Spanish. Results show that a limited prompt produced no meaningful reformulation, and specifications and corpus-informed translations at times showed substantial reformulation, though not always to effect. We find that LLMs can be moved toward reformulation and away from the sentence-by-sentence paradigm, though more work is needed to improve the effectiveness of those reformulations. In this paper, we discuss considerations related to automatic translation system design, corpus construction, and translation quality evaluation methodology and results.

### [121] [Hindcast: Replaying Prediction Markets to Evaluate LLM Forecasters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14051)
*Xiao Ye,Jacob Dineen,Evan Zhu,Shijie Lu,Kevin Song,Ben Zhou*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文针对大模型预测能力的回测评估存在“答案泄露”问题，即模型能通过检索到事件发生后的数据或新模型训练集包含了答案，从而导致回测变成了回忆测试。论文提出“Hindcast”方法，通过冻结在某个历史时点前的Reddit快照，只访问过去的数据，对模型进行严格的前视能力评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前对大模型预测能力的回测往往无法有效区分模型的回忆能力与真实前视推理能力，因为答案会在检索数据或训练数据中泄漏，导致对模型“预测”能力的高估。

Method: 提出Hindcast评估框架：结合Polymarket预测市场的已解决问题，对应冻结的历史Reddit快照，仅允许模型接触$t_0$时点之前的数据，预测后与实际发生及$t_0$时的市场价格（人类预测）进行对比评估。每个市场设独立时间截点，快照数据固定，随着新模型迭代可持续复用。

Result: 分析发现，在“答案泄露”漏洞被彻底封堵后，大部分模型通过检索依然能提升表现，但只有当Reddit讨论过该事件时成立，否则检索反而有害。

Conclusion: Hindcast能够有效杜绝评测中的信息泄漏，真实反映模型前视推理能力。检索对模型预测水平的提升依赖于历史公开讨论数据的丰富程度。

Abstract: Forecasters are evaluated by backtesting, which replays resolved questions and grades the probability the system would have assigned before the outcome was known. For LLMs, two channels leak the answer into this test. A model that retrieves can surface reports written after the event, turning forecasting into a lookup, and each new model is trained on data closer to the event, so a question that lay in the future for last year's models sits inside this year's training data. Either way, the test grades recall while claiming to grade foresight. We introduce Hindcast, which closes both leaks by grading a model as if it stood at a chosen past date $t_0$, before the outcome existed in either channel. Hindcast replays resolved Polymarket prediction markets against a frozen snapshot of public Reddit, lets the model read only posts written before $t_0$, and scores each forecast against both what happened and the market's own price at $t_0$, itself a human forecast made from the same past information. Because the cutoff is set per market and the snapshot never changes, the evaluation re-runs on new markets as models improve, without going stale. Once the leak is closed, retrieval still helps most models, but only where Reddit discussed the event beforehand. Where the archive carried only speculation, retrieval hurts.

</details>

### [122] [Autonomous UAV Route Planning for Coverage Maximization in Environmental Monitoring: A Systematic Literature Review](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13054)
*Sebastian Jouannet-Contreras,Carola Figueroa-Flores*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该论文通过系统性文献综述（SLR）分析了2015-2026年基于覆盖的无人机（UAV）环境监测路径规划相关研究，强调算法类型、能量及覆盖度量、障碍处理等，初步结果揭示该领域研究集中于多无人机协同、能量优化与覆盖优化，对复杂环境关注较少，验证多为仿真。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无人机用于环境监测时，既要覆盖最大区域，又要克服能量和环境约束，对路径规划提出了较高要求。因此，需要对相关研究进行系统综述，梳理现有方法、发展趋势和不足。

Method: 本论文采用PRISMA 2020体系，系统检索Scopus和Web of Science 2015-2026年相关文献，筛查和分析关于路径规划、覆盖路径、信息性路径规划的研究，关注算法、指标、约束等。

Result: 初步筛选401篇文献，247篇进入全文分析。多数文献聚焦覆盖、多UAV协同、能量优化，较少涉及天气、不确定性及大量障碍环境。方法验证多依赖仿真，近年强化学习、混合优化与几何感知路径规划兴趣上升。

Conclusion: 该领域研究活跃但存在碎片化，仿真与现实存在差距，亟需系统化综述来梳理成熟技术与现实环境中的未解难题，促进UAV环境监测任务的实际应用。

Abstract: Environmental monitoring with unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs) requires route planning methods that maximize covered area while handling energy limits, operational constraints, and geometric complexity. This paper reports the protocol and preliminary results of an ongoing systematic literature review (SLR) on autonomous UAV route planning for coverage-oriented environmental monitoring. The review follows the PRISMA 2020 framework and searches Scopus and Web of Science for studies published between 2015 and 2026. The protocol focuses on path planning, coverage path planning, and informative path planning, with emphasis on algorithmic families, coverage and energy metrics, obstacle handling, geometric environment representations, and environmental constraints. At the current stage, 562 records have been identified, 161 duplicates have been removed, and 401 unique records have been screened by title, abstract, and keywords. From these, 247 studies were retained for full-text eligibility assessment (235 eligible and 12 borderline records to be resolved during full-text review). A preliminary analysis of the retained studies suggests strong concentration on coverage-oriented formulations, multi-UAV coordination, and energy-aware optimization, while fewer studies explicitly address weather, uncertainty, or obstacle-rich environments. Most retained studies rely on simulation-based validation, highlighting a potential simulation-to-reality gap, and recent publications show increasing interest in reinforcement learning, hybrid optimization, and geometry-aware planning. These early findings indicate an active but fragmented research landscape and support the need for a structured synthesis to identify mature techniques and unresolved gaps for realistic environmental monitoring missions.

</details>


### [123] [HRIBench: Benchmarking Interaction-Centric Human-Robot Collaboration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13056)
*Chang Liu,Jiawei Zhang,Tao Zhang,Ye Wang,Hongyu Zhou,Qin Jin*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本论文提出了HRIBench基准，专注于人机协作中的意图感知与交互结构，对现有强化操控能力但忽视协作性的机器人系统进行诊断与提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前主流视觉-语言-动作（VLA）基准大多只关注孤立的操控任务，忽略了人机协作所需的意图理解、时序协调和安全交互等核心结构，这限制了机器人在实际合作场景中的应用。

Method: 提出了HRIBench，一个基于可执行交互场景的人机协作基准。HRIBench采用场景剧本建模团队任务，明确区分代理角色、时序依赖、协调约束和人类行为分布，并定义了三类代表性交互角色（指导者、协作者、干扰者），设计了13个基于角色的任务和650多个多样评测场景，引入了同步性、响应性、协议遵从和安全性等可解释交互指标。

Result: 在统一协议下对GR00T、pi0.5和ACT等策略进行评测，结果表明现有机器人策略尽管操控能力强，但在协作性方面表现较差，尤其在时序协调与意图感知方面。HRIBench微调后可显著提升协作表现。实测中HRIBench生成的仿真数据将GR00T N1.5的真实任务成功率从0.10提升到0.43。

Conclusion: HRIBench有效填补了人机协作中意图与交互建模的评测空白，不但揭示了机器人在协作方面的短板，也推动了以交互为中心的机器人学习研究。

Abstract: Current vision-language-action (VLA) benchmarks primarily evaluate isolated manipulation skills while leaving human-robot interaction structure largely unmodeled. However, real-world collaboration fundamentally requires coordination under shared agency, including intent understanding, temporal synchronization, protocol adherence, and safe interaction in dynamic environments. To address this gap, we introduce HRIBench, a diagnostic benchmark for intent-aware human-robot collaboration based on executable interaction scenarios. HRIBench represents collaborative tasks as structured scenario scripts that explicitly model agent roles, temporal dependencies, coordination constraints, and human behavior distributions. Building on this abstraction, HRIBench defines three representative interaction roles: Instructor, Collaborator, and Intruder, covering intent communication, joint coordination, and robustness under human intervention. The benchmark contains 13 role-conditioned tasks with over 650 evaluation episodes generated from diverse interaction trajectories and scene variations. Beyond binary task success, HRIBench introduces interpretable interaction-centric metrics spanning synchronization, responsiveness, protocol compliance, and safety. We evaluate adapted policies based on GR00T, pi0.5, and ACT under a unified protocol. Results show that current foundation robot policies struggle substantially in collaborative settings despite strong manipulation ability, revealing major limitations in temporal coordination and intent-aware behavior. Fine-tuning on HRIBench consistently improves collaborative performance. In a real-world adaptation study, simulation data generated by HRIBench improves GR00T N1.5's physical-task success rate from 0.10 to 0.43, demonstrating the benchmark's value for advancing interaction-centric robot learning.

</details>


### [124] [Power from Potential: A Survey of Electrostatic Actuators for Haptics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13058)
*Ahad M. Rauf,Ran Zhou,Eric Acome,Madeline Balaam,Sean Follmer,Teng Han,Craig Shultz,Daniel Leithinger*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文综述了高压静电驱动器（HVEAs）在触觉技术上的应用，比较了其不同类型的性能，并提出改进方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着触觉接口逐步融入可穿戴设备及日常环境，对柔软、轻薄、静音且低能耗的执行器需求日益增长。传统执行器（如马达和温敏高分子）难以满足这些条件。高压静电驱动器以其特性成为新的研究热点。

Method: 论文聚焦于HVEAs的四大类：可切换静电粘附器、介电弹性体执行器、柔性静电液压执行器和静电动力泵。对每类HVEAs，分析了其驱动机制、带宽、力密度、空间扩展性，并评价其在可穿戴与世界固定型接口中实现触觉反馈的能力。

Result: 通过跨技术对比，论文识别了HVEAs设计中的共性限制，以及提升人体工学、制造和自感应集成的策略。

Conclusion: HVEAs在推动触觉交互方面具有独特潜力，但仍需在实际应用、人体工程学、制造和集成等方面持续研究。

Abstract: As haptic interfaces integrate more seamlessly into wearables and everyday environments, they increasingly require actuators that are soft, thin, silent, and energy efficient. However, conventional motors and temperature-responsive polymers often struggle to deliver these properties due to their bulky form factors and high power consumption. High-Voltage Electrostatic Actuators (HVEAs), which generate force by applying an electric field to localized charge concentrations using high voltages and ultra-low currents, have recently emerged as a compelling alternative due to their fast, silent, and low-power operation within highly customizable and compliant form factors.
  This paper presents a focused review of HVEAs for haptics, examining four major classes: electrostatic switchable adhesives, dielectric elastomer actuators, soft electrohydraulic actuators, and electrokinetic pumps. For each class, we describe their mechanisms that enable haptic output; characterize their bandwidths, force densities, and spatial scalability; and evaluate their versatility for rendering cutaneous and kinesthetic feedback across wearable and world-grounded interfaces. Through this cross-technology analysis, we identify common design constraints and emerging strategies for improving ergonomics, streamlining fabrication, and integrating self-sensing. We conclude by outlining where HVEAs are uniquely positioned to advance haptic interaction and highlighting key research directions needed to translate these technologies into practical systems.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出GPUSimBench基准套件，采用可控斜面任务评估仿真与真实物理动力学的一致性，通过扩展环境数测试吞吐率与内存使用。此外，系统性揭示并量化了GPU批处理导致的非确定性及其对评测一致性的影响，归纳了四种主流模拟栈下的随机性模式。

Result: 实验证明：当前GPU机器人模拟器在大规模并行时表现出显著的运行差异性和随机性，不同环境和多次运行下结果波动大，且物理一致性和可复现性随扩展度提升而劣化。总结了导致不可复现的四种随机性机制。

Conclusion: 为确保具身AI研究的可扩展性与可靠性，未来GPU仿真系统需在扩展能力、物理一致性和计算确定性间实现平衡，并明晰引入随机性的源头和边界。

Abstract: Data-driven embodied AI is rapidly transitioning into a paradigm that scales training through massively parallel simulation, where GPU-accelerated simulators serve as the foundational data infrastructure. However, as computational throughput scales, the underlying trade-offs between parallel efficiency, physical fidelity, and execution determinism remain largely unexamined, hindering the development of reliable robot learning. In this paper, we expose the hidden limits of mainstream GPU-based robotic simulators (e.g., Isaac Lab, Genesis) by introducing GPUSimBench, which focuses on scalability, physical consistency, and computational determinism. First, GPUSimBench establishes a physical grounding evaluation with a controlled inclined-plane task, quantifying the distributional alignment between simulated dynamics and their real-world counterparts. Second, we benchmark parallel scalability by measuring throughput and memory footprints across scaling environment counts. Crucially, beyond standard performance metrics, we unveil and quantify the inherent non-determinism introduced by GPU-batched execution, characterized by significant run-to-run and inter-environment variability even under identical initial conditions. Finally, we identify four empirical regimes of stochasticity within current simulator stacks, highlighting that unbounded scaling can compromise reproducibility without explicit constraints.

### [126] [A Bayesian framework for the uncanny valley in humanoid robot design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13060)
*Shimon Honda,Rin Shibano,Hideyoshi Yanagisawa*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本论文提出用分层贝叶斯生成模型，将“恐怖谷”现象相关的经验性设计指导转化为可操作的算法变量，并通过仿真与实验解释不同变量对人类对类人机器人亲和感的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ‘恐怖谷’效应一直困扰着类人机器人设计，现有的设计指南难以转化为可操作的算法变量，限制了基于算法的机器人外貌与行为优化。

Method: 作者构建了分层贝叶斯生成模型，将恐怖谷机制归纳为四个设计变量（类别均值偏离、跨模态一致性、人类相似性预测不确定性、观察不确定性），并通过仿真和机器人--人类变形图像的人类被试实验验证模型预测。

Result: 仿真结果显示类别模糊与外貌-动作失配能显著降低亲和感，不确定性会改变恐怖谷的形状。实验中，增加观察不确定性减弱了中间相似性区间熟悉感的下降，而降低预测不确定性提升了更像机器人的外貌评分。

Conclusion: 该框架首次将恐怖谷的经验性设计启示转化为可用于算法优化的数学变量，为类人机器人外貌与行为的计算设计和优化提供了理论基础和操作性工具。

Abstract: The uncanny valley is a long-standing empirical rule in humanoid robot design: making robots more human-like can reduce, rather than increase, affinity. Yet existing guidelines, such as adopting robot-like appearances, avoiding excessive realism, and reducing cross-modal mismatches, remain difficult to use for algorithmic design because they are not expressed as manipulable variables. Here, we propose a hierarchical Bayesian generative model that operationalizes these guidelines as mathematical design variables. The model represents affinity toward humanoid robots as posterior-weighted negative category-conditional surprise and explains category ambiguity and perceptual mismatch as increases in surprise. It maps uncanny-valley mechanisms onto four variables: deviation from the predicted robot-category mean, inconsistency in human likeness across modalities, prediction uncertainty, and observational uncertainty. Simulations showed that category ambiguity and appearance--motion mismatch can produce affinity reductions, and that uncertainty reshapes the valley. In a human-subject experiment with robot--human morphing images, we manipulated prediction uncertainty using blurred prior robot stimuli and observational uncertainty using blurred evaluation stimuli. Increased observational uncertainty attenuated the decrease in familiarity ratings at intermediate human likeness, whereas low prediction uncertainty increased ratings for robot-like appearances. This framework turns empirical uncanny-valley heuristics into a computational basis for algorithmically evaluating and optimizing humanoid robot appearance and behavior.

### [127] [A 3DGS-Driven Dynamic Viewpoint and Vibrotactile Framework for Subsea Teleoperation Validated via fNIRS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13067)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Teleoperating remotely operated vehicles (ROVs) in flooded, cluttered infrastructure is fundamentally limited by narrow 2D egocentric views and subsea communication latency. We present a multimodal teleoperation architecture built on a ROS-Unity framework that decouples proactive spatial planning from reactive boundary avoidance. The system replaces static camera feeds with a Dynamic Adaptive Viewpoint System (DAVS), which uses continuous optimization and real-time 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) to synthesize an occlusion-free exocentric viewpoint from onboard state estimation. To further reduce sensory workload, a torso-mounted vibrotactile suit maps local obstacle clearance to intuitive haptic proximity cues. The architecture was evaluated in a controlled human-subject study (N = 30) using a BlueROV2 navigating a complex simulated underwater facility. A 3 x 4 repeated-measures design compared three interaction modalities (Egocentric, Haptic, Exocentric) under four communication delays (0.0-1.0 s). Performance was quantified using behavioral measures and functional near-infrared spectroscopy (fNIRS) to assess task-evoked prefrontal activation. Results show that reactive haptic feedback improves path adherence under minimal delay, whereas the 3DGS-driven exocentric visualization provides superior resilience under severe latency (0.5-1.0 s), significantly outperforming the other modalities. fNIRS further revealed a cognitive disengagement effect: increasing latency during conventional egocentric teleoperation overloaded working memory and reduced prefrontal activation, whereas the proactive spatial context provided by DAVS sustained executive control. These findings demonstrate that spatially grounded, multimodal assistance can substantially improve operator performance and cognitive endurance during latency-degraded underwater teleoperation.

### [129] [Worlds in One Demo: A Synthetic Data Engine for Learning Open-World Mobile Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13154)
*Lingxiao Guo,Huanyu Li,Guanya Shi*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: WANDA系统通过合成数据引擎，仅需单次人类演示即可大幅扩展移动操作机器人的数据集，实现泛化和鲁棒性的提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的遥操作和UMI等数据采集方式严重依赖人力，难以大规模生成覆盖各种场景和变化的数据。为突破人工收集的瓶颈，需要寻找能够极大提升每次人类演示价值的方法，从而推动在开放世界中移动操作任务的学习和泛化。

Method: WANDA首先根据RGBD数据重建环境背景和机器人-物体交互轨迹，再将这些交互片段进行空间重组，通过全身运动规划生成新轨迹。采用状态纠正扩展技术，丰富机器人及物体在移动操作各阶段的状态分布，为跨环境泛化，在多样化的3D虚拟世界中合成新轨迹。采用高质量渲染将机器人与物体复合于背景，实现照片级视图合成，最终自动化大规模合成训练数据。

Result: 经过大规模模拟和真实场景实验验证，使用WANDA训练的策略在长时序任务鲁棒性、空间泛化和跨环境泛化上表现优异。同时，WANDA支持不同机器人形态的数据迁移，实现新机器人上的零样本部署。

Conclusion: WANDA极大提高了每次人类演示的利用率，实现了高效、经济的数据生成和泛化能力，为开放世界移动操作学习提供了新范式，并展现了跨机器人平台无缝迁移的潜力。

Abstract: Learning open-world mobile manipulation policies requires vast data to achieve spatial generalization, long-horizon robustness, and scene generalization.
